<Author>PT68
<Content>A perfect small hotel I can't say enough good things about this hotel. I traveled to Paris with my parents and my partner, and my father came down with a bad flu not long after we arrived. The Varenne staff was outstanding, helping us get in touch with a doctor (doctors in Paris make house calls, and come with an hour!), and taking care of all of our extra needs (finding a pharmacist, etc.). The hotel is completely cozy, and everything is spotless. Rooms and bathrooms are just the right size. Beds are very comfortable. Nice flat-screen tvs. The breakfast was delicious (although all of those carbs so early in the morning can make for sleepy sightseeing). I couldn't imagine staying at a better place in this price range.The location is quite pleasant, although somewhat of a walk to more entertaining areas. Also, it's just about impossible to find a restaurant (or anything) open on Sunday, and next to impossible to find a restaurant open on a Saturday night. I would advise against using taxis if you can help it -- we found that the drivers took many indirect routes and added on all sorts of hidden fees.

What a perfect little Paris hotel! We loved the quiet, out of the way location. First you pass through a garden courtyard  enter the dignified lobby. The staff is helpful  speaks excellent English. It's only 2 blocks from the Metro  there are a grocery, bakery  restaurants plus museums close by.We had a very clean superior twin room, decorated in Neo-classical style which was as large as most US hotel rooms. The Varenne was recently renovated. The plumbing, tile  decoration are brand new  the rooms have a fridge, safe, cable TV  AC. The towels are nice  fluffy. We got a special summer rate with breakfast, so every morning we enjoyed hot chocolate  warm chocolate croissants in the courtyard--heavenly!The only negatives were the tiny elevator  the scaffold outside our window (but the workmen only worked weekdays, so weekends were quiet. Hopefully when you stay at the Varenne the scaffold will be gone.) Also our telephone didn't work very well.This is a great hotel for honeymooneers  romantics. Also, for women traveling alone, since the neighborhood feels very safe. The only improvement I can suggest would be a little vase of fresh flowers in my room  chocolates on the pillow--or is that too much of a cliche?  
<Date>Sep 13, 2005

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Charming! INSIDE: Just renovated. Clean everywhere (bath room, carpet etc), nice interior, new towels, TV provided NHK, CNN, BBC and others. Suite and non-suite rooms are not too much difference (we stayed both). The rooms with windows facing the hotel's garden are better than the ones facing the street. Both types had safe, refrig., hair dryer, shampoo  shower gel. We did not use internet because they charge 6 euro per hour (or first hour, I don't remember). I wish they had bigger pillows (it maybe an American thing to have big and/or many pillows).OUTSIDE: Nice and quiet surrounded by govermental offices, super charming corridor and garding with table and chairs (we had wine, cheese and bread and sat there for 3 hours to enjoy conversation. hotel provided glasses, bottle opener, napkins!). SERVICE: Everybody spoke English except maids. Very friendly. Quick responses via e-mails. Nice breadfast comes with orange juice, croissant, chololate croissant, baguette, jam, butter, coffee (non-expresso) or hot cholocate. LOCATION: Hotel is at Metro M13 Varenne station. If you are coming from the CDG using Metro/RER, you will take RER B (30 min), switch at St. Michell to RER C, get off at Invalides and walk to the hotel or switch to Metro 13 to go to Varenne. Note Metro stations do not have escalators or elevators. To and from Varenne station, you can view Eiffel tower (beautiful at night!)PRICE: Go to the home page to find out any promotion. We paid 129 euro for suite and 119 for non-suite.I definately recommend Varenne if you want to stay in clean, quiet, nice but not intimidating place.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>An absolutely outstanding hotel in Paris This is, without a doubt, the best Paris hotel I have ever stayed in, and certainly one of the best small hotels I've stayed in anywhere. The rooms are spacious, immaculately clean and have loads of light. The breakfast served downstairs each morning is fantastic - fresh croissants and baguette and wonderful cafe au lait. The location is perfect: within walking distance of the Champs Elysees and the Eiffel Tower, in Les Invalides.But it is the staff that deserves special mention. Everyone is courteous and helpful - indeed, they really do go the extra mile to be helpful -- to the point that they mailed two t-shirts that I had forgotten in our room to me. Even little things like checking when the local post office opens or locating a local laundry for me - it has been a long time since I received such excellent service in a hotel.I will not hesitate to return to the Hotel de Varenne the next time I am in Paris and highly recommend it to anyone looking for a wonderful small hotel that is centrally located.

<Author>hstraveler
<Content>Great value, clean and quiet Most of what I have to say has been said before in the numerous reviews. The location is good, but not exactly ideal. You can walk to 3 museums: d'Orsay, Rodin, and les Invalides, which is nice, but the closest metro station isn't a major one so you'll have to transfer a lot. Its on a quiet street and the rooms are very clean and well maintained. The bathroom is big by European standards, but like many French hotels, there is no shower curtain or door so you have to be careful not to soak the bathroom when bathing. Breakfast in the courtyard was very relaxing and good, but don't expect an American breakfast. Its just a basket of really good breads and jams, OJ, and coffee, tea or hot chocolate. I didn't find the staff overly friendly, but they definitely were not rude or anything. They have WiFi in the rooms, but you have to buy a fairly expensive access card. Even the lobby PC has a fee to use the internet. There's a good bakery a few doors down and a small grocery store across the street. Several restaurants are within a 5-10 min. walk.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>It's all true I want to thank all of those who have left reviews of this hotel before me, great recommendations and I would recommend this place to anyone. Great value, good sized rooms, nice flat-screen TV with good range of European / UK channels, air conditioning that worked well in a mini-heat wave, and the staff are friendly and speak good English. Location is peaceful but very central, only a few minutes walk from the metro or the RER. The safe worked (I find sometimes they don't, or they are temperamental so I dont trust them in case all my thing get locked and I can't get them). Lots of nice touches that you don't always get in this class of hotel: eg about a dozen good quality removeable wooden coat hangers in a wardrobe (I hate those hangers that you can't remove from the rail and are impossible to use sometimes). A couple of minor points.....a bit stingey with towels (1 small bath towel, 1 hand towel and 1 floor towel), maybe it's because I was staying in the room alone I only got this number, but an extra towel would have been appreciated. Had it been an issue I'd have asked for an extra towel, the staff are very approachable so don't think it would have been an issue....I didn't see any smoke detectors, and there is no fire door separating a corridor of rooms from the main stairway / lobby. I am sure it meets whatever standards there are, and maybe there are smoke detectors, but I'd have felt reassured to see a smoke detector hard-wired in the ceiling of my room and in the corridor. I felt safe (and was on 1st floor), but the fire safety precautions are thigns I am always aware of when I stay away, and comment on when I post reviews here - maybe someone else staying at the hotel can provide more information on this. Overall a real gem of a place, wish there were more like it and I'm certainly going to return (as long as it's not always fully booked because of all these good reviews!).  
<Date>Jul 18, 2005

<Author>manilagirl
<Content>Hotel de Varenne: A Great Find Visited Paris recently with my husband and son. And we are so lucky to have decided to stay at Hotel de Varenne (thanks to Trip Advisor reviews). Loved the Hotel. Our room was super clean, super cool (with airconditioning that looked new to me) and big enough for 3 people (me, my husband and 12 year-old son). And the bathroom was really elegant and squeaky clean! The extra bed was a real bed not a rollaway or folding bed which other hotels provide. What more, they had a pretty garden where we had breakfast every morning and which really gave me a high after a tiring day. We also enjoyed the breakfast of soft and warm bread, and yummy hot chocolat. The hotel is also located in a very quiet place (embassy row) and for people like me who prefer to go to a place that's quiet after a hectic and tiring day, this is the hotel for me. It's so convenient to reach anyway because it is just 200 meters away from a metro station (Varenne). And there is a mini grocery at the corner and a bakery that sells very good croissant right beside the hotel. I also found the staff very friendly. And what makes it more amazing is the hotel rate which is very reasonable compared to other hotels. I would go back to this hotel and recommend it to my family and friends!
